events-chat 2022-02-23 01:43:26 ```PCC Zeppelin Event```



**Who can join?**
Anyone can join, they just have to build a ship of a certain class and submit it to the event-submissions to hopefully be chosen.

**Defenders VS Invaders** 
Your Team captains will be, **Shepdog11fpss, and Rbk321** 
when the round ends you will switch, alternating roles.
There are 3 Classes of ships for you to chose from. 

```Explanation: ```
The PCC Zeppelin event will consist of two teams fighting eachother, almost like the previous event. This time though there will be a dreadnought classed ship on the defending side, and on the opposing team there shall be a frigate. With the dreadnought and frigate there will be 3 sub classes for people to play as. More simply on the attacking side there will be 3 ships with one frigate, and on the defending side a dreadnought with 3 ships. 

```RESTRICTIONS```
(These are for the ships that you guys will be creating)
No TNT armor
Fireworks, and Lava Spitters are NOT allowed
Glitches/bug abusing is prohibited
Only Propeller engines form the prefab menu , or Custom prop engines that are made from motors, pistons, hover engines, and other forms of blocks that can produce movement shall be allowed
Speakers are prohibited

Cutters are allowed for the torpedo boat allowing them to be used to ram into other ships, or to be used on the torpedoes. 

 You can Motor lock outside of the build area as long as it does not make your airship massively overpowered | I, and a few others will inspect your ship when the time is ready to make sure this rule will not be breached in any way . For more clarity if you were to chose a destroyer class then you can motorlock outside of your limit to then condense it into the limit.
